Started abcSGP Saturday March 25 00:03:19 2023


	abcSGP(
		 sgp_object = SGP_object
		state = state.abbr
		steps = c("analyzeSGP", "combineSGP")
		sgp.percentiles = TRUE
		sgp.projections = FALSE
		sgp.projections.lagged = FALSE
		sgp.percentiles.baseline = FALSE
		sgp.projections.baseline = FALSE
		sgp.projections.lagged.baseline = FALSE
		sgp.use.my.coefficient.matrices = if (is.null(coef_matrices)) NULL else TRUE
		simulate.sgps = FALSE
		goodness.of.fit.print = FALSE
		parallel.config = list(BACKEND = "PARALLEL", WORKERS = workers)
		sgp.config = config )


Started analyzeSGP Saturday March 25 00:03:19 2023


	analyzeSGP(
		 sgp_object = sgp_object
		state = state
		years = years
		content_areas = content_areas
		grades = grades
		sgp.percentiles = sgp.percentiles
		sgp.projections = sgp.projections
		sgp.projections.lagged = sgp.projections.lagged
		sgp.percentiles.baseline = sgp.percentiles.baseline
		sgp.projections.baseline = sgp.projections.baseline
		sgp.projections.lagged.baseline = sgp.projections.lagged.baseline
		sgp.minimum.default.panel.years = sgp.minimum.default.panel.years
		sgp.use.my.coefficient.matrices = sgp.use.my.coefficient.matrices
		sgp.test.cohort.size = sgp.test.cohort.size
		return.sgp.test.results = return.sgp.test.results
		simulate.sgps = simulate.sgps
		calculate.simex = calculate.simex
		calculate.simex.baseline = calculate.simex.baseline
		calculate.srs = calculate.srs
		calculate.srs.baseline = calculate.srs.baseline
		goodness.of.fit.print = goodness.of.fit.print
		sgp.config = sgp.config
		parallel.config = parallel.config
		verbose.output = verbose.output
		get.cohort.data.info = get.cohort.data.info
		sgp.sqlite = sgp.sqlite
		sgp.percentiles.equated = sgp.percentiles.equated
		sgp.percentiles.equating.method = sgp.percentiles.equating.method
		sgp.percentiles.calculate.sgps = sgp.percentiles.calculate.sgps
		SGPt = SGPt
		fix.duplicates = fix.duplicates )

	abcSGP(
		 sgp_object = SGP_object
		state = state.abbr
		steps = c("analyzeSGP", "combineSGP")
		sgp.percentiles = TRUE
		sgp.projections = FALSE
		sgp.projections.lagged = FALSE
		sgp.percentiles.baseline = FALSE
		sgp.projections.baseline = FALSE
		sgp.projections.lagged.baseline = FALSE
		sgp.use.my.coefficient.matrices = if (is.null(coef_matrices)) NULL else TRUE
		simulate.sgps = FALSE
		goodness.of.fit.print = FALSE
		parallel.config = list(BACKEND = "PARALLEL", WORKERS = workers)
		sgp.config = config )


Started analyzeSGP Saturday March 25 01:26:38 2023


	analyzeSGP(
		 sgp_object = sgp_object
		state = state
		years = years
		content_areas = content_areas
		grades = grades
		sgp.percentiles = sgp.percentiles
		sgp.projections = sgp.projections
		sgp.projections.lagged = sgp.projections.lagged
		sgp.percentiles.baseline = sgp.percentiles.baseline
		sgp.projections.baseline = sgp.projections.baseline
		sgp.projections.lagged.baseline = sgp.projections.lagged.baseline
		sgp.minimum.default.panel.years = sgp.minimum.default.panel.years
		sgp.use.my.coefficient.matrices = sgp.use.my.coefficient.matrices
		sgp.test.cohort.size = sgp.test.cohort.size
		return.sgp.test.results = return.sgp.test.results
		simulate.sgps = simulate.sgps
		calculate.simex = calculate.simex
		calculate.simex.baseline = calculate.simex.baseline
		calculate.srs = calculate.srs
		calculate.srs.baseline = calculate.srs.baseline
		goodness.of.fit.print = goodness.of.fit.print
		sgp.config = sgp.config
		parallel.config = parallel.config
		verbose.output = verbose.output
		get.cohort.data.info = get.cohort.data.info
		sgp.sqlite = sgp.sqlite
		sgp.percentiles.equated = sgp.percentiles.equated
		sgp.percentiles.equating.method = sgp.percentiles.equating.method
		sgp.percentiles.calculate.sgps = sgp.percentiles.calculate.sgps
		SGPt = SGPt
		fix.duplicates = fix.duplicates )

Started abcSGP Saturday March 25 01:44:12 2023


	abcSGP(
		 sgp_object = SGP_object
		state = state.abbr
		steps = c("analyzeSGP", "combineSGP")
		sgp.percentiles = TRUE
		sgp.projections = FALSE
		sgp.projections.lagged = FALSE
		sgp.percentiles.baseline = FALSE
		sgp.projections.baseline = FALSE
		sgp.projections.lagged.baseline = FALSE
		sgp.use.my.coefficient.matrices = if (is.null(coef_matrices)) NULL else TRUE
		simulate.sgps = FALSE
		goodness.of.fit.print = FALSE
		parallel.config = list(BACKEND = "PARALLEL", WORKERS = workers)
		sgp.config = config )


Started analyzeSGP Saturday March 25 01:44:12 2023


	analyzeSGP(
		 sgp_object = sgp_object
		state = state
		years = years
		content_areas = content_areas
		grades = grades
		sgp.percentiles = sgp.percentiles
		sgp.projections = sgp.projections
		sgp.projections.lagged = sgp.projections.lagged
		sgp.percentiles.baseline = sgp.percentiles.baseline
		sgp.projections.baseline = sgp.projections.baseline
		sgp.projections.lagged.baseline = sgp.projections.lagged.baseline
		sgp.minimum.default.panel.years = sgp.minimum.default.panel.years
		sgp.use.my.coefficient.matrices = sgp.use.my.coefficient.matrices
		sgp.test.cohort.size = sgp.test.cohort.size
		return.sgp.test.results = return.sgp.test.results
		simulate.sgps = simulate.sgps
		calculate.simex = calculate.simex
		calculate.simex.baseline = calculate.simex.baseline
		calculate.srs = calculate.srs
		calculate.srs.baseline = calculate.srs.baseline
		goodness.of.fit.print = goodness.of.fit.print
		sgp.config = sgp.config
		parallel.config = parallel.config
		verbose.output = verbose.output
		get.cohort.data.info = get.cohort.data.info
		sgp.sqlite = sgp.sqlite
		sgp.percentiles.equated = sgp.percentiles.equated
		sgp.percentiles.equating.method = sgp.percentiles.equating.method
		sgp.percentiles.calculate.sgps = sgp.percentiles.calculate.sgps
		SGPt = SGPt
		fix.duplicates = fix.duplicates )

	abcSGP(
		 sgp_object = SGP_object
		state = state.abbr
		steps = c("analyzeSGP", "combineSGP")
		sgp.percentiles = TRUE
		sgp.projections = FALSE
		sgp.projections.lagged = FALSE
		sgp.percentiles.baseline = FALSE
		sgp.projections.baseline = FALSE
		sgp.projections.lagged.baseline = FALSE
		sgp.use.my.coefficient.matrices = if (is.null(coef_matrices)) NULL else TRUE
		simulate.sgps = FALSE
		goodness.of.fit.print = FALSE
		parallel.config = list(BACKEND = "PARALLEL", WORKERS = workers)
		sgp.config = config )


Started analyzeSGP Saturday March 25 02:01:46 2023


	analyzeSGP(
		 sgp_object = sgp_object
		state = state
		years = years
		content_areas = content_areas
		grades = grades
		sgp.percentiles = sgp.percentiles
		sgp.projections = sgp.projections
		sgp.projections.lagged = sgp.projections.lagged
		sgp.percentiles.baseline = sgp.percentiles.baseline
		sgp.projections.baseline = sgp.projections.baseline
		sgp.projections.lagged.baseline = sgp.projections.lagged.baseline
		sgp.minimum.default.panel.years = sgp.minimum.default.panel.years
		sgp.use.my.coefficient.matrices = sgp.use.my.coefficient.matrices
		sgp.test.cohort.size = sgp.test.cohort.size
		return.sgp.test.results = return.sgp.test.results
		simulate.sgps = simulate.sgps
		calculate.simex = calculate.simex
		calculate.simex.baseline = calculate.simex.baseline
		calculate.srs = calculate.srs
		calculate.srs.baseline = calculate.srs.baseline
		goodness.of.fit.print = goodness.of.fit.print
		sgp.config = sgp.config
		parallel.config = parallel.config
		verbose.output = verbose.output
		get.cohort.data.info = get.cohort.data.info
		sgp.sqlite = sgp.sqlite
		sgp.percentiles.equated = sgp.percentiles.equated
		sgp.percentiles.equating.method = sgp.percentiles.equating.method
		sgp.percentiles.calculate.sgps = sgp.percentiles.calculate.sgps
		SGPt = SGPt
		fix.duplicates = fix.duplicates )

	prepareSGP(
		 data = resampleData(sgp_data, config)
		state = state.abbr
		create.additional.variables = FALSE )

	NOTE: All values of observed data reside within the LOSS/HOSS values in the SGPstateData meta-data for GA.
	NOTE: All values of observed data reside within the BOUNDARY values in the SGPstateData meta-data for GA.
	NOTE: YEAR in @Data converted from integer to character.
	NOTE: GRADE in @Data converted from integer to character.
	NOTE: SCALE_SCORE in @Data converted from integer to numeric.
Finished prepareSGP Saturday March 25 02:19:22 2023 in 15.664 Seconds 


Started abcSGP Saturday March 25 02:19:22 2023


	abcSGP(
		 sgp_object = SGP_object
		state = state.abbr
		steps = c("analyzeSGP", "combineSGP")
		sgp.percentiles = TRUE
		sgp.projections = FALSE
		sgp.projections.lagged = FALSE
		sgp.percentiles.baseline = FALSE
		sgp.projections.baseline = FALSE
		sgp.projections.lagged.baseline = FALSE
		sgp.use.my.coefficient.matrices = if (is.null(coef_matrices)) NULL else TRUE
		simulate.sgps = FALSE
		goodness.of.fit.print = FALSE
		parallel.config = list(BACKEND = "PARALLEL", WORKERS = workers)
		sgp.config = config )


Started analyzeSGP Saturday March 25 02:19:22 2023


	analyzeSGP(
		 sgp_object = sgp_object
		state = state
		years = years
		content_areas = content_areas
		grades = grades
		sgp.percentiles = sgp.percentiles
		sgp.projections = sgp.projections
		sgp.projections.lagged = sgp.projections.lagged
		sgp.percentiles.baseline = sgp.percentiles.baseline
		sgp.projections.baseline = sgp.projections.baseline
		sgp.projections.lagged.baseline = sgp.projections.lagged.baseline
		sgp.minimum.default.panel.years = sgp.minimum.default.panel.years
		sgp.use.my.coefficient.matrices = sgp.use.my.coefficient.matrices
		sgp.test.cohort.size = sgp.test.cohort.size
		return.sgp.test.results = return.sgp.test.results
		simulate.sgps = simulate.sgps
		calculate.simex = calculate.simex
		calculate.simex.baseline = calculate.simex.baseline
		calculate.srs = calculate.srs
		calculate.srs.baseline = calculate.srs.baseline
		goodness.of.fit.print = goodness.of.fit.print
		sgp.config = sgp.config
		parallel.config = parallel.config
		verbose.output = verbose.output
		get.cohort.data.info = get.cohort.data.info
		sgp.sqlite = sgp.sqlite
		sgp.percentiles.equated = sgp.percentiles.equated
		sgp.percentiles.equating.method = sgp.percentiles.equating.method
		sgp.percentiles.calculate.sgps = sgp.percentiles.calculate.sgps
		SGPt = SGPt
		fix.duplicates = fix.duplicates )

		 sgp_object = sgp_object
		state = state
		years = years
		content_areas = content_areas
		grades = grades
		sgp.percentiles = sgp.percentiles
		sgp.projections = sgp.projections
		sgp.projections.lagged = sgp.projections.lagged

		sgp.minimum.default.panel.years = sgp.minimum.default.panel.years
		sgp.use.my.coefficient.matrices = sgp.use.my.coefficient.matrices
		sgp.test.cohort.size = sgp.test.cohort.size
		return.sgp.test.results = return.sgp.test.results
		simulate.sgps = simulate.sgps
		calculate.simex = calculate.simex
		calculate.simex.baseline = calculate.simex.baseline
		calculate.srs = calculate.srs
		calculate.srs.baseline = calculate.srs.baseline

		fix.duplicates = fix.duplicates )

Started abcSGP Saturday March 25 04:00:20 2023


	abcSGP(
		 sgp_object = SGP_object
		state = state.abbr
		steps = c("analyzeSGP", "combineSGP")
		sgp.percentiles = TRUE
		sgp.projections = FALSE
		sgp.projections.lagged = FALSE
		sgp.percentiles.baseline = FALSE
		sgp.projections.baseline = FALSE
		sgp.projections.lagged.baseline = FALSE
		sgp.use.my.coefficient.matrices = if (is.null(coef_matrices)) NULL else TRUE
		simulate.sgps = FALSE
		goodness.of.fit.print = FALSE
		parallel.config = list(BACKEND = "PARALLEL", WORKERS = workers)
		sgp.config = config )


Started analyzeSGP Saturday March 25 04:00:20 2023


	analyzeSGP(
		 sgp_object = sgp_object
		state = state
		years = years
		content_areas = content_areas
		grades = grades
		sgp.percentiles = sgp.percentiles
		sgp.projections = sgp.projections
		sgp.projections.lagged = sgp.projections.lagged
		sgp.percentiles.baseline = sgp.percentiles.baseline
		sgp.projections.baseline = sgp.projections.baseline
		sgp.projections.lagged.baseline = sgp.projections.lagged.baseline
		sgp.minimum.default.panel.years = sgp.minimum.default.panel.years
		sgp.use.my.coefficient.matrices = sgp.use.my.coefficient.matrices
		sgp.test.cohort.size = sgp.test.cohort.size
		return.sgp.test.results = return.sgp.test.results
		simulate.sgps = simulate.sgps
		calculate.simex = calculate.simex
		calculate.simex.baseline = calculate.simex.baseline
		calculate.srs = calculate.srs
		calculate.srs.baseline = calculate.srs.baseline
		goodness.of.fit.print = goodness.of.fit.print
		sgp.config = sgp.config
		parallel.config = parallel.config
		verbose.output = verbose.output
		get.cohort.data.info = get.cohort.data.info
		sgp.sqlite = sgp.sqlite
		sgp.percentiles.equated = sgp.percentiles.equated
		sgp.percentiles.equating.method = sgp.percentiles.equating.method
		sgp.percentiles.calculate.sgps = sgp.percentiles.calculate.sgps
		SGPt = SGPt
		fix.duplicates = fix.duplicates )

	abcSGP(
		 sgp_object = SGP_object
		state = state.abbr
		steps = c("analyzeSGP", "combineSGP")
		sgp.percentiles = TRUE
		sgp.projections = FALSE
		sgp.projections.lagged = FALSE
		sgp.percentiles.baseline = FALSE
		sgp.projections.baseline = FALSE
		sgp.projections.lagged.baseline = FALSE
		sgp.use.my.coefficient.matrices = if (is.null(coef_matrices)) NULL else TRUE
		simulate.sgps = FALSE
		goodness.of.fit.print = FALSE
		parallel.config = list(BACKEND = "PARALLEL", WORKERS = workers)
		sgp.config = config )


Started analyzeSGP Saturday March 25 04:17:55 2023


	analyzeSGP(
		 sgp_object = sgp_object
		state = state
		years = years
		content_areas = content_areas
		grades = grades
		sgp.percentiles = sgp.percentiles
		sgp.projections = sgp.projections
		sgp.projections.lagged = sgp.projections.lagged
		sgp.percentiles.baseline = sgp.percentiles.baseline
		sgp.projections.baseline = sgp.projections.baseline
		sgp.projections.lagged.baseline = sgp.projections.lagged.baseline
		sgp.minimum.default.panel.years = sgp.minimum.default.panel.years
		sgp.use.my.coefficient.matrices = sgp.use.my.coefficient.matrices
		sgp.test.cohort.size = sgp.test.cohort.size
		return.sgp.test.results = return.sgp.test.results
		simulate.sgps = simulate.sgps
		calculate.simex = calculate.simex
		calculate.simex.baseline = calculate.simex.baseline
		calculate.srs = calculate.srs
		calculate.srs.baseline = calculate.srs.baseline
		goodness.of.fit.print = goodness.of.fit.print
		sgp.config = sgp.config
		parallel.config = parallel.config
		verbose.output = verbose.output
		get.cohort.data.info = get.cohort.data.info
		sgp.sqlite = sgp.sqlite
		sgp.percentiles.equated = sgp.percentiles.equated
		sgp.percentiles.equating.method = sgp.percentiles.equating.method
		sgp.percentiles.calculate.sgps = sgp.percentiles.calculate.sgps
		SGPt = SGPt
		fix.duplicates = fix.duplicates )

Started abcSGP Saturday March 25 04:35:28 2023


	abcSGP(
		 sgp_object = SGP_object
		state = state.abbr
		steps = c("analyzeSGP", "combineSGP")
		sgp.percentiles = TRUE
		sgp.projections = FALSE
		sgp.projections.lagged = FALSE
		sgp.percentiles.baseline = FALSE
		sgp.projections.baseline = FALSE
		sgp.projections.lagged.baseline = FALSE
		sgp.use.my.coefficient.matrices = if (is.null(coef_matrices)) NULL else TRUE
		simulate.sgps = FALSE
		goodness.of.fit.print = FALSE
		parallel.config = list(BACKEND = "PARALLEL", WORKERS = workers)
		sgp.config = config )


Started analyzeSGP Saturday March 25 04:35:28 2023


	analyzeSGP(
		 sgp_object = sgp_object
		state = state
		years = years
		content_areas = content_areas
		grades = grades
		sgp.percentiles = sgp.percentiles
		sgp.projections = sgp.projections
		sgp.projections.lagged = sgp.projections.lagged
		sgp.percentiles.baseline = sgp.percentiles.baseline
		sgp.projections.baseline = sgp.projections.baseline
		sgp.projections.lagged.baseline = sgp.projections.lagged.baseline
		sgp.minimum.default.panel.years = sgp.minimum.default.panel.years
		sgp.use.my.coefficient.matrices = sgp.use.my.coefficient.matrices
		sgp.test.cohort.size = sgp.test.cohort.size
		return.sgp.test.results = return.sgp.test.results
		simulate.sgps = simulate.sgps
		calculate.simex = calculate.simex
		calculate.simex.baseline = calculate.simex.baseline
		calculate.srs = calculate.srs
		calculate.srs.baseline = calculate.srs.baseline
		goodness.of.fit.print = goodness.of.fit.print
		sgp.config = sgp.config
		parallel.config = parallel.config
		verbose.output = verbose.output
		get.cohort.data.info = get.cohort.data.info
		sgp.sqlite = sgp.sqlite
		sgp.percentiles.equated = sgp.percentiles.equated
		sgp.percentiles.equating.method = sgp.percentiles.equating.method
		sgp.percentiles.calculate.sgps = sgp.percentiles.calculate.sgps
		SGPt = SGPt
		fix.duplicates = fix.duplicates )

	analyzeSGP(
		 sgp_object = sgp_object
		state = state
		years = years
		content_areas = content_areas
		grades = grades
		sgp.percentiles = sgp.percentiles
		sgp.projections = sgp.projections
		sgp.projections.lagged = sgp.projections.lagged

		sgp.projections.lagged.baseline = sgp.projections.lagged.baseline
		sgp.minimum.default.panel.years = sgp.minimum.default.panel.years
		sgp.use.my.coefficient.matrices = sgp.use.my.coefficient.matrices
		sgp.test.cohort.size = sgp.test.cohort.size
		return.sgp.test.results = return.sgp.test.results
		simulate.sgps = simulate.sgps
		calculate.simex = calculate.simex
		calculate.simex.baseline = calculate.simex.baseline
		calculate.srs = calculate.srs
		calculate.srs.baseline = calculate.srs.baseline
		goodness.of.fit.print = goodness.of.fit.print

		verbose.output = verbose.output
		get.cohort.data.info = get.cohort.data.info

		sgp.percentiles.equating.method = sgp.percentiles.equating.method
		sgp.percentiles.calculate.sgps = sgp.percentiles.calculate.sgps
		SGPt = SGPt
		fix.duplicates = fix.duplicates )

Started abcSGP Saturday March 25 06:16:34 2023


	abcSGP(
		 sgp_object = SGP_object
		state = state.abbr
		steps = c("analyzeSGP", "combineSGP")
		sgp.percentiles = TRUE
		sgp.projections = FALSE
		sgp.projections.lagged = FALSE
		sgp.percentiles.baseline = FALSE
		sgp.projections.baseline = FALSE
		sgp.projections.lagged.baseline = FALSE
		sgp.use.my.coefficient.matrices = if (is.null(coef_matrices)) NULL else TRUE
		simulate.sgps = FALSE
		goodness.of.fit.print = FALSE
		parallel.config = list(BACKEND = "PARALLEL", WORKERS = workers)
		sgp.config = config )


Started analyzeSGP Saturday March 25 06:16:34 2023


	analyzeSGP(
		 sgp_object = sgp_object
		state = state
		years = years
		content_areas = content_areas
		grades = grades
		sgp.percentiles = sgp.percentiles
		sgp.projections = sgp.projections
		sgp.projections.lagged = sgp.projections.lagged
		sgp.percentiles.baseline = sgp.percentiles.baseline
		sgp.projections.baseline = sgp.projections.baseline
		sgp.projections.lagged.baseline = sgp.projections.lagged.baseline
		sgp.minimum.default.panel.years = sgp.minimum.default.panel.years
		sgp.use.my.coefficient.matrices = sgp.use.my.coefficient.matrices
		sgp.test.cohort.size = sgp.test.cohort.size
		return.sgp.test.results = return.sgp.test.results
		simulate.sgps = simulate.sgps
		calculate.simex = calculate.simex
		calculate.simex.baseline = calculate.simex.baseline
		calculate.srs = calculate.srs
		calculate.srs.baseline = calculate.srs.baseline
		goodness.of.fit.print = goodness.of.fit.print
		sgp.config = sgp.config
		parallel.config = parallel.config
		verbose.output = verbose.output
		get.cohort.data.info = get.cohort.data.info
		sgp.sqlite = sgp.sqlite
		sgp.percentiles.equated = sgp.percentiles.equated
		sgp.percentiles.equating.method = sgp.percentiles.equating.method
		sgp.percentiles.calculate.sgps = sgp.percentiles.calculate.sgps
		SGPt = SGPt
		fix.duplicates = fix.duplicates )
